{
  "command": "node -e \"\nconst { execSync } = require('child_process');\nconst dbPath = require('os').homedir() + '/.local/share/opencode/opencode.db';\nconst sessionId = 'ses_2a13d4153ffeJHdMrZE0rexV13';\nconst lastProcessedUuid = 'msg_d63120ec4001aiMEWwokXRkCsV_tool_toolu_01FS9QLp1UAYeasnSLzaor87';\n\n// Read and normalize messages (simplified from the ETM code)\nconst query = \\`SELECT m.id, m.time_created, m.data as msg_data, GROUP_CONCAT(p.data, '|||PART_SEP|||') as parts_data FROM message m LEFT JOIN part p ON p.message_id = m.id WHERE m.session_id = '\\${sessionId}' GROUP BY m.id ORDER BY m.time_created ASC;\\`;\nconst result = execSync(\\`sqlite3 -separator '|||COL_SEP|||' \\\"\\${dbPath}\\\" \\\"\\${query}\\\"\\`, { encoding: 'utf-8', timeout: 15000, maxBuffer: 50*1024*1024 }).trim();\n\nconst normalized = [];\nfor (const row of result.split('\\n')) {\n  if (!row.trim()) continue;\n  const cols = row.split('|||COL_SEP|||');\n  if (cols.length < 3) continue;\n  const msgId = cols[0];\n  const timeCreated = cols[1];\n  let msgData;\n  try { msgData = JSON.parse(cols[2]); } catch { continue; }\n  const partsRaw = cols.length > 3 ? cols[3] : '';\n  const parts = partsRaw ? partsRaw.split('|||PART_SEP|||').map(p => { try { return JSON.parse(p); } catch { return null; } }).filter(Boolean) : [];\n  const timestamp = new Date(parseInt(timeCreated, 10)).toISOString();\n\n  if (msgData.role === 'user') {\n    const textParts = parts.filter(p => p.type === 'text');\n    const userText = textParts.map(p => p.text || '').join('\\n') || '';\n    normalized.push({ type: 'user', uuid: msgId, timestamp, message: { role: 'user', content: [{ type: 'text', text: userText }] } });\n  } else if (msgData.role === 'assistant') {\n    const content = [];\n    for (const part of parts) {\n      if (part.type === 'text' && part.text) {\n        content.push({ type: 'text', text: part.text });\n      } else if (part.type === 'tool' && part.tool && part.state) {\n        content.push({ type: 'tool_use', id: part.callID || part.tool, name: part.tool, input: part.state?.input || {} });\n        if (part.state?.status === 'completed' && part.state?.output != null) {\n          const resultContent = typeof part.state.output === 'string' ? part.state.output : JSON.stringify(part.state.output);\n          normalized.push({ type: 'assistant', uuid: msgId, timestamp, message: { role: 'assistant', content: [...content], stop_reason: 'tool_use' } });\n          content.length = 0;\n          normalized.push({ type: 'user', uuid: msgId + '_tool_' + (part.callID || part.tool), timestamp, message: { role: 'user', content: [{ type: 'tool_result', tool_use_id: part.callID || part.tool, content: resultContent.substring(0, 50000) }] } });\n          continue;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    if (content.length > 0) {\n      normalized.push({ type: 'assistant', uuid: msgId, timestamp, message: { role: 'assistant', content, stop_reason: msgData.finish || 'end_turn' } });\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n// Find lastProcessedUuid index\nconst lpIdx = normalized.findIndex(m => m.uuid === lastProcessedUuid);\nconsole.log('Total normalized:', normalized.length);\nconsole.log('lastProcessedUuid index:', lpIdx);\n\nif (lpIdx >= 0) {\n  const remaining = normalized.slice(lpIdx + 1);\n  console.log('Remaining messages:', remaining.length);\n  \n  // Count actual user prompts in remaining\n  let userPrompts = 0;\n  let toolResults = 0;\n  for (const m of remaining) {\n    if (m.type === 'user' && m.message?.role === 'user') {\n      const isToolResult = m.message.content.some(item => item.type === 'tool_result' && item.tool_use_id);\n      if (isToolResult) {\n        toolResults++;\n      } else {\n        userPrompts++;\n        console.log('USER PROMPT found:', m.uuid, m.message.content[0]?.text?.substring(0, 80));\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  console.log('User prompts:', userPrompts);\n  console.log('Tool results:', toolResults);\n}\n\" 2>&1",
  "description": "Debug: trace extractExchanges on OpenCode data",
  "timeout": 30000
}

An exchange is unprocessed if its lastMessageUuid\n    // comes after lastProcessedUuid in the message stream.\n    let unprocessed;\n\n    if (!this.lastProcessedUuid) {\n      unprocessed = exchanges.slice(-10);\n    } else {\n      // Find which message lastProcessedUuid corresponds to\n      const lastProcessedMsgIndex = messages.findIndex(msg => msg.uuid === this.lastProcessedUuid);\n      if (lastProcessedMsgIndex >= 0) {\n        // Find exchanges that contain messages AFTER lastProcessedUuid.\n        // An exchange is unprocessed if its lastMessageUuid is after lastProcessedMsgIndex.\n        unprocessed = exchanges.filter(ex => {\n          const exLastUuid = ex.lastMessageUuid || ex.id;\n          const exMsgIndex = messages.findIndex(m => m.uuid === exLastUuid);\n          return exMsgIndex > lastProcessedMsgIndex;\n        });\n        this.debug(`🔍 Found ${unprocessed.length} unprocessed exchanges (${unprocessed.filter(e => e.isUserPrompt).length} user prompts) after msg index ${lastProcessedMsgIndex}`);\n      } else {\n        // UUID not found in messages, fall back to last 10 exchanges\n        this.debug(`⚠️ lastProcessedUuid not found in messages, using last 10 exchanges`);\n        unprocessed = exchanges.slice(-10);\n      }\n    }\n\n    return unprocessed;"
}
```

to capture assistant responses and tool results\n    if (unprocessed.length === 0 && lastProcessedMsgIndex >= 0) {\n      const messagesAfter = messages.slice(lastProcessedMsgIndex + 1);\n      if (messagesAfter.length > 0) {\n        const firstMsgAfter = messagesAfter[0];\n        const isUserPrompt = firstMsgAfter.type === 'user' &&\n          firstMsgAfter.message?.role === 'user' &&\n          !this.isToolResultMessage(firstMsgAfter);\n\n        if (!isUserPrompt) {\n          // Create continuation exchange manually\n          const continuationExchange = {\n            id: firstMsgAfter.uuid || `continuation_${Date.now()}`,\n            timestamp: firstMsgAfter.timestamp || new Date().toISOString(),\n            userMessage: '',\n            claudeResponse: '',\n            toolCalls: [],\n            toolResults: [],\n            isUserPrompt: false,\n            isComplete: true,  // FIX: Continuation exchanges ARE complete - they contain accumulated content\n            stopReason: 'continuation',\n            isContinuation: true,\n            lastMessageUuid: firstMsgAfter.uuid\n          };\n\n          // Accumulate content from all messages after lastProcessedUuid\n          for (const msg of messagesAfter) {\n            if (msg.type === 'assistant' && msg.message?.content) {\n              if (Array.isArray(msg.message.content)) {\n                for (const item of msg.message.content) {\n                  if (item.type === 'text') {\n                    continuationExchange.claudeResponse += item.text + '\\n';\n                  } else if (item.type === 'tool_use') {\n                    continuationExchange.toolCalls.push({\n                      name: item.name,\n                      input: item.input,\n                      id: item.id\n                    });\n                  }\n                }\n              }\n              if (msg.uuid) continuationExchange.lastMessageUuid = msg.uuid;\n            } else if (msg.type === 'user' && msg.message?.content && Array.isArray(msg.message.content)) {\n              for (const item of msg.message.content) {\n                if (item.type === 'tool_result') {\n                  continuationExchange.toolResults.push({\n                    tool_use_id: item.tool_use_id,\n                    content: item.content,\n                    is_error: item.is_error || false\n                  });\n                }\n              }\n              if (msg.uuid) continuationExchange.lastMessageUuid = msg.uuid;\n            }\n          }\n\n          this.debug(`📎 Created continuation exchange from ${messagesAfter.length} messages after lastProcessedUuid`);\n          unprocessed = [continuationExchange];\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Return all unprocessed exchanges - filtering moved to processUserPromptSetCompletion\n    return unprocessed;",
  "new_string": "    // Filter to unprocessed exchanges using the FULL exchange list (which correctly\n    // splits on user prompts). An exchange is unprocessed if its lastMessageUuid\n    // comes after lastProcessedUuid in the message stream.\n    let unprocessed;\n\n    if (!this.lastProcessedUuid) {\n      unprocessed = exchanges.slice(-10);\n    } else {\n      // Find which message lastProcessedUuid corresponds to\n      const lastProcessedMsgIndex = messages.findIndex(msg => msg.uuid === this.lastProcessedUuid);\n      if (lastProcessedMsgIndex >= 0) {\n        // Find exchanges that contain messages AFTER lastProcessedUuid.\n        // An exchange is unprocessed if its lastMessageUuid is after lastProcessedMsgIndex.\n        unprocessed = exchanges.filter(ex => {\n          const exLastUuid = ex.lastMessageUuid || ex.id;\n          const exMsgIndex = messages.findIndex(m => m.uuid === exLastUuid);\n          return exMsgIndex > lastProcessedMsgIndex;\n        });\n        this.debug(`🔍 Found ${unprocessed.length} unprocessed exchanges (${unprocessed.filter(e => e.isUserPrompt).length} user prompts) after msg index ${lastProcessedMsgIndex}`);\n      } else {\n        // UUID not found in messages, fall back to last 10 exchanges\n        this.debug(`⚠️ lastProcessedUuid not found in messages, using last 10 exchanges`);\n        unprocessed = exchanges.slice(-10);\n      }\n    }\n\n    return unprocessed;"
}
